### [419] [Learning to Think from Multiple Thinkers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24737)
*Nirmit Joshi,Roey Magen,Nathan Srebro,Nikolaos Tsilivis,Gal Vardi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文研究了从多个思考者提供的思维链监督中学习的问题，证明了在某些情况下从少数思考者的思维链数据中学习是困难的，但提出了一种高效的主动学习算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究如何利用多个思考者提供的正确但可能系统不同的思维链监督进行学习，例如不同思考者解决数学问题的逐步解法，或不同程序解决同一问题的执行轨迹。

Method: 通过理论分析，在密码学假设下证明从两个或少数思考者的思维链监督中学习可能是困难的。同时提出一种通用的计算高效的主动学习算法，该算法需要少量每个思考者的思维链数据、中等数量的思考者，以及足够的被动结果监督数据。

Result: 在被动数据收集设置下，从两个或少数不同思考者的思维链监督中学习可能是困难的。但提出的主动学习算法能够以独立于目标精度ε的少量每个思考者思维链数据、中等数量的思考者（对数规模），以及多项式对数规模的结果监督数据进行高效学习。

Conclusion: 从多个思考者的思维链监督中学习具有理论上的挑战性，特别是在被动设置下。但通过主动学习方法，可以高效地利用多个思考者的思维链信息，实现比仅使用结果监督更有效的学习。

Abstract: We study learning with Chain-of-Thought (CoT) supervision from multiple thinkers, all of whom provide correct but possibly systematically different solutions, e.g., step-by-step solutions to math problems written by different thinkers, or step-by-step execution traces of different programs solving the same problem.
  We consider classes that are computationally easy to learn using CoT supervision from a single thinker, but hard to learn with only end-result supervision, i.e., without CoT (Joshi et al. 2025). We establish that, under cryptographic assumptions, learning can be hard from CoT supervision provided by two or a few different thinkers, in passive data-collection settings.
  On the other hand, we provide a generic computationally efficient active learning algorithm that learns with a small amount of CoT data per thinker that is completely independent of the target accuracy $\varepsilon$, a moderate number of thinkers that scales as $\log \frac{1}{\varepsilon}\log \log \frac{1}{\varepsilon}$, and sufficient passive end-result data that scales as $\frac{1}{\varepsilon}\cdot poly\log\frac{1}{\varepsilon}$.

</details>


### [420] [Conflict-Aware Harmonized Rotational Gradient for Multiscale Kinetic Regimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24745)
*Zhangyong Liang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出HRGrad方法，通过协调梯度处理多尺度动力学问题中的梯度冲突，确保多任务同时训练


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多尺度时间依赖动力学问题中，小参数从微观到宏观的渐近转变导致多任务学习困难，不同渐近区域的求解任务常出现梯度冲突，导致多任务学习失败

Method: 提出HRGrad方法：1) 显式编码参数的隐表示，使求解任务序列化同时训练；2) 分割预测结果构建任务损失；3) 引入新梯度对齐度量确保最终更新与各损失特定梯度的点积为正，保持所有任务损失优化率一致并基于冲突水平动态调整梯度大小

Result: 在BGK方程和线性输运方程的所有Knudsen数范围内进行广泛实验，结果表明HRGrad有效克服了APNNs在这些问题中的"失效模式"

Conclusion: HRGrad方法通过数学证明收敛性，能有效解决多尺度动力学问题中的梯度冲突，为渐近保持神经网络在多参数范围同时训练提供了可行方案

Abstract: In this paper, we propose a harmonized rotational gradient method, termed HRGrad, for simultaneously tackling multiscale time-dependent kinetic problems with varying small parameters.
  These parameters exhibit asymptotic transitions from microscopic to macroscopic physics, making it a challenging multi-task problem to solve over all ranges simultaneously.
  Solving tasks in different asymptotic regions often encounter gradient conflicts, which can lead to the failure of multi-task learning.
  To address this challenge, we explicitly encode a hidden representation of these parameters, ensuring that the corresponding solving tasks are serialized for simultaneous training.
  Furthermore, to mitigate gradient conflicts, we segment the prediction results to construct task losses and introduce a novel gradient alignment metric to ensure a positive dot product between the final update and each loss-specific gradient.
  This metric maintains consistent optimization rates for all task losses and dynamically adjusts gradient magnitudes based on conflict levels.
  Moreover, we provide a mathematical proof demonstrating the convergence of the HRGrad method, which is evaluated across a range of challenging asymptotic-preserving neural networks (APNNs) scenarios.
  We conduct an extensive set of experiments encompassing the Bhatnagar-Gross-Krook (BGK) equation and the linear transport equation in all ranges of Knudsen number.
  Our results indicate that HRGrad effectively overcomes the `failure modes' of APNNs in these problems.

</details>


### [421] [The Optimal Sample Complexity of Multiclass and List Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24749)
*Chirag Pabbaraju*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文解决了多类分类样本复杂度的开放问题，证明了Daniely和Shalev-Shwartz的长期猜想，确定了DS维度的最优样本复杂度


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多类分类的最优样本复杂度问题长期未解决，尽管二元分类的样本复杂度（基于VC维度）已有定论，但多类分类的DS维度存在√DS的上下界差距

Method: 基于Hanneke等人（2026）的多类假设类DS维度代数表征，证明了多类假设类的最大超图密度上界由其DS维度决定

Result: 证明了Daniely和Shalev-Shwartz（2014）的长期猜想，确定了多类分类和列表学习中DS维度的最优样本复杂度

Conclusion: 该工作解决了多类分类样本复杂度的基本开放问题，为多类学习理论提供了重要理论突破

Abstract: While the optimal sample complexity of binary classification in terms of the VC dimension is well-established, determining the optimal sample complexity of multiclass classification has remained open. The appropriate complexity parameter for multiclass classification is the DS dimension, and despite significant efforts, a gap of $\sqrt{\text{DS}}$ has persisted between the upper and lower bounds on sample complexity.
  Recent work by Hanneke et al. (2026) shows a novel algebraic characterization of multiclass hypothesis classes in terms of their DS dimension. Building up on this, we show that the maximum hypergraph density of any multiclass hypothesis class is upper-bounded by its DS dimension. This proves a longstanding conjecture of Daniely and Shalev-Shwartz (2014). As a consequence, we determine the optimal dependence of the sample complexity on the DS dimension for multiclass as well as list learning.

</details>
